conn = sqlite3.connect('/home/user/Desktop/exodus-kali-deploy/dialer.db')
conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
cursor = conn.cursor()
try:
    cursor.execute('''
        SELECT id, phone_number, reason, created_at
        FROM dnc_list
        ORDER BY created_at DESC
        LIMIT 1
    ''')
    print('DNC query works')
except Exception as e:
    print(f'DNC error: {e}')

try:
    cursor.execute('''
        SELECT 
            l.id, l.phone_number, l.first_name, l.last_name,
            l.email, l.company, l.status, l.last_called,
            c.name as campaign_name
        FROM leads l
        LEFT JOIN campaigns c ON l.campaign_id = c.id
        ORDER BY l.created_at DESC
        LIMIT 1
    ''')
    print('Leads query works')

[DEBUG] Bash tool invoked with command: python3 << 'EOF'
import sqlite3
import asyncio
import aiosqlite

async def test():
    db = await aiosqlite.connect('dialer.db')
    db.row_factory = aiosqlite.Row
    
    query = """
        SELECT * FROM leads
        WHERE campaign_id = ?
        AND status IN ('NEW', 'CALLBACK')
        AND (next_call_time IS NULL OR next_call_time <= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP)
        LIMIT 10
    """
    
    async with db.execute(query, (20,)) as cursor:
        rows = await cursor.fetchall()
        print(f"Found {len(rows)} leads:")
        for row in rows:
            print(dict(row)['id'], dict(row)['phone_number'], dict(row)['status'])
    
    await db.close()

asyncio.run(test())
EOF
